Link: https://yugioh.fandom.com/wiki/List_of_Yu-Gi-Oh!_Duel_Generation_cards


This is a  list of cards in  Yu-Gi-Oh! Duel Generation  (Game ver. 106a for Android/ver. 2.010 for iOS). The game features more than 7000 playable cards and 96 tokens, numbered from 3900 to 12432; the number does not start from number 0 or 1. Over 1000 numbers were omitted.  Below is a list of the cards in the game, these cards may be removed in the future. If a card is removed, please do not remove it, simply state that the card is removed. 
 A  gallery of cards  can also be viewed.
